msg:The check-in lobby is on the 7th floor, where there is a sky garden with flowers, trees, small bridges and flowing water. You can overlook the People's Park downstairs and the Jining Museum in the distance. (It takes about 20 minutes to walk there) It is very close to Taibai Tower, and there is also a "Cixiao Jianwanfang" which is a royal memorial archway and very impressive.
The hotel is clean and the bedding is tidy. There is an indoor swimming pool on the 8th floor, which is free for guests to use. Swimsuits can also be purchased at the entrance. There are Chinese food, Western food and barbecue.
